<script>
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
  document.querySelectorAll('td a[href*="raw.githubusercontent.com"]').forEach(function(a) {
    a.style.cursor = 'pointer';
    a.title = '点击复制链接';
    a.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
      e.preventDefault();
      var url = this.href;
      navigator.clipboard.writeText(url).then(function() {
        var orig = a.textContent;
        a.textContent = '✅ 已复制!';
        a.style.color = '#22c55e';
        setTimeout(function() { a.textContent = orig; a.style.color = ''; }, 1500);
      });
    });
  });
});
</script>
